    expect(mockSyncOnSignIn).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
  });

  it("starts sync once when a user is present", () => {
    mockUseSession.mockReturnValue({ user: { id: "u1" } } as unknown as ReturnType<typeof useSession>);
    renderHook(() => useSync());
    expect(mockSubscribe).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
    expect(mockSyncOnSignIn).toHaveBeenCalledWith("u1");
  });

  it("cleans up (unsubscribe + flush) on unmount", () => {
    const unsubscribe = jest.fn();
    mockSubscribe.mockReturnValue(unsubscribe);
    mockUseSession.mockReturnValue({ user: { id: "u1" } } as unknown as ReturnType<typeof useSession>);

    const { unmount } = renderHook(() => useSync());
    unmount();

    expect(unsubscribe).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
    expect(mockFlush).toHaveBeenCalled();
  });
});

- [ ] **Step 2: Run test to verify it fails**

Command: `npm run test -- src/features/sync/use-sync.test.ts`
Expected failure: `Cannot find module '@/src/features/sync/use-sync'`.

- [ ] **Step 3: Write minimal implementation** (complete)

Create `src/features/sync/use-sync.ts`:
```ts
import { useEffect, useRef } from "react";

import { signInWithGoogle } from "@/src/features/auth/api";
import {
  flushPendingPushes,
  scheduleBackgroundPush,
  syncOnSignIn,
} from "@/src/features/sync/orchestrator";
import { syncBus } from "@/src/lib/sync-bus";
import { useSession } from "@/src/providers/session-provider";

/**
 * Begin sync for a signed-in user: subscribe the sync-bus (every change notification
 * schedules a debounced push) and run the full sign-in merge once. Returns a cleanup
 * that unsubscribes and flushes any pending pushes. Sync failures are logged, not thrown.
 */
export function startSyncForUser(userId: string): () => void {
  const unsubscribe = syncBus.subscribe((sessionId) => {
    scheduleBackgroundPush(userId, sessionId);
  });

  void syncOnSignIn(userId).catch((error) => {
    console.warn("[sync] syncOnSignIn failed", error);
  });

  return () => {
    unsubscribe();
    void flushPendingPushes();
  };
}

/**
 * Kick off Google sign-in from the "Sign in to sync" button or the (auth) flow.
 * Sync itself starts reactively in useSync when `user` becomes non-null (covering
 * both the web redirect-callback path and native in-app completion).
 */
export async function runSyncSignIn(): Promise<void> {
  await signInWithGoogle();
}

/** Mount once high in the tree: starts/stops sync as auth state flips. */
export function useSync(): void {
  const { user } = useSession();
  const cleanupRef = useRef<(() => void) | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!user) return;

    cleanupRef.current = startSyncForUser(user.id);
    return () => {
      cleanupRef.current?.();
      cleanupRef.current = null;
    };
  }, [user]);
}
```

- [ ] **Step 4: Run test to verify it passes**

Command: `npm run test -- src/features/sync/use-sync.test.ts`
Expected: PASS — bus-subscribe-schedules-push, kicks-off-syncOnSignIn, cleanup-unsubscribe-flush, runSyncSignIn-starts-google, and the three `useSync` lifecycle cases green.

- [ ] **Step 5: Commit**

```bash
git add src/features/sync/use-sync.ts src/features/sync/use-sync.test.ts
git commit -m "feat(sync): use-sync wires orchestrator to auth state + sync-bus

Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 <noreply@anthropic.com>"
```

### Task P7.11: Mount `useSync` in app providers

**Files:**

- Test: `src/providers/app-providers.test.tsx`

**Interfaces:**
- Consumes: `useSync` from `@/src/features/sync/use-sync`.
- Produces: a `<SyncGate>` child rendered INSIDE `SessionProvider` (so `useSession()` is available) that calls `useSync()` once and renders its children. This makes the whole app drive sync from one mount point without a route change. No new exported symbols other than the internal gate.

- [ ] **Step 1: Write the failing test** (complete) — verifies the providers tree mounts `useSync` exactly once.

```ts
// src/providers/app-providers.test.tsx
import { render } from "@testing-library/react-native";
import { Text } from "react-native";

import { AppProviders } from "@/src/providers/app-providers";
import { useSync } from "@/src/features/sync/use-sync";

jest.mock("@/src/features/sync/use-sync", () => ({ useSync: jest.fn() }));

const mockUseSync = jest.mocked(useSync);

describe("AppProviders", () => {
  beforeEach(() => jest.clearAllMocks());

  it("renders children", () => {
    const { getByText } = render(
      <AppProviders>
        <Text>hello</Text>
      </AppProviders>,
    );
    expect(getByText("hello")).toBeTruthy();
  });

  it("mounts the sync gate (calls useSync once)", () => {
    render(
      <AppProviders>
        <Text>hello</Text>
      </AppProviders>,
    );
    expect(mockUseSync).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
  });
});
```

- [ ] **Step 2: Run test to verify it fails**

Command: `npm run test -- src/providers/app-providers.test.tsx`
Expected failure: `expect(mockUseSync).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1)` fails with received `0` (gate not yet wired into the tree).

- [ ] **Step 3: Write minimal implementation** — add a `SyncGate` inside `SessionProvider`. Read the current file first; the edit inserts the gate so it wraps `children` within `SessionProvider`. The final relevant region of `src/providers/app-providers.tsx`:

```tsx
import type { PropsWithChildren } from "react";
import { SafeAreaProvider } from "react-native-safe-area-context";
import { QueryClient, QueryClientProvider } from "@tanstack/react-query";

import { I18nProvider } from "@/src/providers/i18n-provider";
import { SessionProvider } from "@/src/providers/session-provider";
import { useSync } from "@/src/features/sync/use-sync";

const queryClient = new QueryClient();

/** Lives inside SessionProvider so useSession() resolves; drives sync as auth state flips. */
function SyncGate({ children }: PropsWithChildren) {
  useSync();
  return <>{children}</>;
}

export function AppProviders({ children }: PropsWithChildren) {
  return (
    <SafeAreaProvider>
      <QueryClientProvider client={queryClient}>
        <I18nProvider>
          <SessionProvider>
            <SyncGate>{children}</SyncGate>
          </SessionProvider>
        </I18nProvider>
      </QueryClientProvider>
    </SafeAreaProvider>
  );
}
```
(Preserve any additional providers already present in the Phase 1 file — only insert `SyncGate` as the innermost wrapper inside `SessionProvider` and add the `useSync` import + `SyncGate` definition. Do not remove existing providers.)

- [ ] **Step 4: Run test to verify it passes**

Command: `npm run test -- src/providers/app-providers.test.tsx`
Expected: PASS — children render and `useSync` is invoked once.

- [ ] **Step 5: Commit**

```bash
git add src/providers/app-providers.tsx src/providers/app-providers.test.tsx
git commit -m "feat(sync): mount useSync via SyncGate inside SessionProvider

Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 <noreply@anthropic.com>"
```

```tsx
// src/features/canvas/CanvasScreen.sync.test.tsx
import { render } from "@testing-library/react-native";

import { CanvasScreen } from "@/src/features/canvas/CanvasScreen";
import { syncSessionOnOpen } from "@/src/features/sync/orchestrator";
import { useSession } from "@/src/providers/session-provider";
import { useSessionBundle } from "@/src/features/sessions/queries";

jest.mock("@/src/features/sync/orchestrator", () => ({ syncSessionOnOpen: jest.fn() }));
jest.mock("@/src/providers/session-provider", () => ({ useSession: jest.fn() }));
jest.mock("@/src/features/sessions/queries", () => ({
  useSessionBundle: jest.fn(),
  useUpdateViewport: jest.fn(() => ({ mutate: jest.fn() })),
  useUpdateNodeGeometry: jest.fn(() => ({ mutate: jest.fn() })),
  useAddNode: jest.fn(() => ({ mutateAsync: jest.fn() })),
  useAddEdge: jest.fn(() => ({ mutateAsync: jest.fn() })),
}));
// CanvasBoard pulls Skia/gesture-handler; stub it to a no-op so the screen renders in jest.
jest.mock("@/src/features/canvas/CanvasBoard", () => ({ CanvasBoard: () => null }));

const mockSyncOnOpen = jest.mocked(syncSessionOnOpen);
const mockUseSession = jest.mocked(useSession);
const mockUseSessionBundle = jest.mocked(useSessionBundle);

const bundle = {
  session: {
    id: "s1",
    userId: "u1",
    title: "T",
    viewportX: 0,
    viewportY: 0,
    viewportZoom: 1,
    createdAt: "c",
    updatedAt: "u",
    deletedAt: null,
  },
  nodes: [{ id: "n1", sessionId: "s1", articleTitle: "T", lang: "en", x: 0, y: 0, width: 380, height: 520, parentNodeId: null, createdAt: "c" }],
  edges: [],
};

describe("CanvasScreen — syncSessionOnOpen wiring", () => {
  beforeEach(() => {
    jest.clearAllMocks();
    mockSyncOnOpen.mockResolvedValue(undefined);
    mockUseSessionBundle.mockReturnValue({
      data: bundle,
      isLoading: false,
      isError: false,
      error: null,
    } as unknown as ReturnType<typeof useSessionBundle>);
  });

  it("syncs the open session when a user is signed in", () => {
    mockUseSession.mockReturnValue({ user: { id: "u1" } } as unknown as ReturnType<typeof useSession>);
    render(<CanvasScreen sessionId="s1" />);
    expect(mockSyncOnOpen).toHaveBeenCalledWith("u1", "s1");
  });

  it("does not sync when signed out", () => {
    mockUseSession.mockReturnValue({ user: null } as unknown as ReturnType<typeof useSession>);
    render(<CanvasScreen sessionId="s1" />);
    expect(mockSyncOnOpen).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
  });
});
```

- [ ] **Step 2: Run test to verify it fails**

- [ ] **Step 3: Write minimal implementation** — read `src/features/canvas/CanvasScreen.tsx`, then add imports + one effect. Do NOT redeclare `screenWidth`/`screenHeight`/`updateViewport` (Phase 4/5 own them).

Add imports (with existing imports):
```tsx
import { useEffect } from "react"; // merge into existing react import if present
import { syncSessionOnOpen } from "@/src/features/sync/orchestrator";
import { useSession } from "@/src/providers/session-provider";
```
Add inside the component body (alongside existing hooks; `user` is a new local, not a redeclaration of an existing one — if `useSession` is already consumed, reuse the existing `user` and add only the effect):
```tsx
const { user } = useSession();

// Pull + merge this session from remote when it opens while signed in. Fire-and-forget:
// a sync failure must never block opening the canvas. (spec §9/§11)
useEffect(() => {
  if (!user) return;
  void syncSessionOnOpen(user.id, sessionId).catch((error) => {
    console.warn("[sync] syncSessionOnOpen failed", error);
  });
}, [user, sessionId]);
```

### Task P7.15: Sync e2e (mocked Supabase) — anon → sign-in → adopt → merge

**Files:**
- Create: `test/e2e/sync.e2e.test.ts`

**Interfaces:**
- Consumes: the platform-agnostic LocalStore seed convention (V2: write ROW-shape snake_case objects into the PLURAL IndexedDB stores `sessions`/`nodes`/`edges`); the `sign-in-sync` button testID (P7.12); a mocked `supabase` (route-intercepted) and a mocked `signInWithGoogle` that synthesizes a signed-in session. Playwright config from Phase 1.
- Produces: an e2e proving the local-first → sync handoff: seed an anonymous session locally, intercept the auth + REST calls so sign-in resolves to a known `user_id` and the remote returns one extra session, press "Sign in to sync", and assert both the adopted local session and the downloaded remote session are visible. This screen/canvas behavior is covered by e2e (not the ratchet), per the spec testing strategy.

- [ ] **Step 1: Write the failing test** (complete)

```ts
// test/e2e/sync.e2e.test.ts
import { test, expect, type Page } from "@playwright/test";

const ANON_SESSION = {
  id: "00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000001",
  user_id: null,
  title: "Local Roman Empire",
  viewport_x: 0,
  viewport_y: 0,
  viewport_zoom: 1,
  created_at: "2026-01-01T00:00:00.000Z",
  updated_at: "2026-01-01T00:00:00.000Z",
  deleted_at: null,
};
const ANON_NODE = {
  id: "00000000-0000-0000-0000-0000000000a1",
  session_id: ANON_SESSION.id,
  article_title: "Roman Empire",
  lang: "en",
  x: 0,
  y: 0,
  width: 380,
  height: 520,
  parent_node_id: null,
  created_at: "2026-01-01T00:00:00.000Z",
};
const REMOTE_SESSION = {
  id: "00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000002",
  user_id: "user-xyz",
  title: "Remote Byzantine Empire",
  viewport_x: 0,
  viewport_y: 0,
  viewport_zoom: 1,
  created_at: "2026-02-01T00:00:00.000Z",
  updated_at: "2026-02-01T00:00:00.000Z",
  deleted_at: null,
};

/** Seed one anonymous session as ROW objects into the PLURAL IndexedDB stores (V2 seed convention). */
async function seedAnonSession(page: Page) {
  await page.addInitScript(
    ({ session, node }) => {
      const open = indexedDB.open("wikicanvas", 1);
      open.onsuccess = () => {
        const db = open.result;
        const tx = db.transaction(["sessions", "nodes"], "readwrite");
        tx.objectStore("sessions").put(session);
        tx.objectStore("nodes").put(node);
      };
    },
    { session: ANON_SESSION, node: ANON_NODE },
  );
}

/** Intercept Supabase REST so sign-in resolves and the remote returns one extra session. */
async function mockSupabase(page: Page) {
  await page.route("**/rest/v1/session**", (route) => {
    if (route.request().method() === "GET") {
      return route.fulfill({
        status: 200,
        contentType: "application/json",
        body: JSON.stringify([REMOTE_SESSION]),
      });
    }
    // upserts (POST/PATCH) just succeed
    return route.fulfill({ status: 200, contentType: "application/json", body: "[]" });
  });
  await page.route("**/rest/v1/node**", (route) =>
    route.fulfill({ status: 200, contentType: "application/json", body: "[]" }),
  );
  await page.route("**/rest/v1/edge**", (route) =>
    route.fulfill({ status: 200, contentType: "application/json", body: "[]" }),
  );
  // Stub the auth flow: pressing sign-in injects a fake signed-in session.
  await page.addInitScript(() => {
    (window as unknown as { __WIKICANVAS_FAKE_USER__?: string }).__WIKICANVAS_FAKE_USER__ =
      "user-xyz";
  });
}

test.describe("auth-gated sync", () => {
  test("anonymous session is adopted and remote session is downloaded on sign-in", async ({
    page,
  }) => {
    await mockSupabase(page);
    await seedAnonSession(page);

    await page.goto("/");

    // Anonymous local session is visible with no login.
    await expect(page.getByText("Local Roman Empire")).toBeVisible();

    // Trigger sign-in -> sync.
    await page.getByTestId("sign-in-sync").click();

    // After merge: the remote-only session is now present locally too.
    await expect(page.getByText("Remote Byzantine Empire")).toBeVisible();
    // The adopted anonymous session is still present.
    await expect(page.getByText("Local Roman Empire")).toBeVisible();
  });
});
```

- [ ] **Step 2: Run test to verify it fails**

Command: `npm run test:e2e -- sync.e2e.test.ts`
Expected failure: the assertion `getByText("Remote Byzantine Empire")` times out — sign-in/sync handoff is not yet observable end-to-end (or the page/seed needs the wiring from prior tasks). This red establishes the integration gap.

- [ ] **Step 3: Write minimal implementation** — make the e2e observable. Two small, test-only seams (no production logic change beyond what prior tasks added):
  1. Confirm the `sign-in-sync` button is rendered for anonymous users (P7.12) and that pressing it begins the sync flow.
  2. Add a tiny test hook so the mocked browser can complete sign-in without a real Google round-trip. In `src/features/sync/use-sync.ts`, `runSyncSignIn` already calls `signInWithGoogle`; for e2e, allow an injected fake user to short-circuit:

```ts
// --- in src/features/sync/use-sync.ts, replace runSyncSignIn with this e2e-aware version ---
import { startSyncForUser as _startSyncForUser } from "@/src/features/sync/use-sync"; // (illustrative; same module)

export async function runSyncSignIn(): Promise<void> {
  const fakeUser = (globalThis as { __WIKICANVAS_FAKE_USER__?: string }).__WIKICANVAS_FAKE_USER__;
  if (fakeUser) {
    // e2e/test seam: skip the real OAuth redirect and start sync directly.
    startSyncForUser(fakeUser);
    return;
  }
  await signInWithGoogle();
}
```
(Use the in-module `startSyncForUser` directly — drop the illustrative self-import; it is shown only to indicate the function is the same one defined above in this file. The production path is unchanged: when `__WIKICANVAS_FAKE_USER__` is unset, it calls `signInWithGoogle` exactly as before.)

Because `applyMergeResult` writes the downloaded `REMOTE_SESSION` into the local store and `adoptAnonSessions` stamps the anon one, the sessions list (which reads from the local store via `useSessionsList`) re-renders with both titles after `syncOnSignIn` completes. If `useSessionsList` is not auto-invalidated post-sync, add one line at the end of `startSyncForUser`'s `syncOnSignIn` success to nudge a refetch via the existing `syncBus`/query invalidation already used by mutations — but prefer relying on the local-store read path the list already uses. (No change to `queries.ts` is permitted; if a refresh is needed, dispatch through `syncBus.notify` is NOT appropriate for a pull — instead, the list query should be invalidated by the screen's own focus/refetch already wired in Phase 6.)

- [ ] **Step 4: Run test to verify it passes**

Command: `npm run test:e2e -- sync.e2e.test.ts`
Expected: PASS — anonymous "Local Roman Empire" visible pre-sign-in; after clicking `sign-in-sync`, "Remote Byzantine Empire" appears and "Local Roman Empire" remains.

- [ ] **Step 5: Commit**

```bash
git add test/e2e/sync.e2e.test.ts src/features/sync/use-sync.ts
git commit -m "test(sync): e2e anon adopt + remote download on sign-in (mocked Supabase)

Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 <noreply@anthropic.com>"
```
